7.  _Thanks for that. Have you heard_ _if anyone else has noticed this_, | _or if this driver has been involved in_ _any other incidents_?
    感谢您的信息。您知道有没有其他人也注意到这事，| 或者这个司机还有没有发生过别的事故？

8.  好多邻居都看到过呢，| 对他都快闻风丧胆了。| 他开车像疯了一样快，| 我们都很担心孩子们的安全。
    _Plenty of our neighbours_ _have seen him too_ | _and are almost_ _scared stiff of him_. | _He drives insanely fast_, | _and we're all really worried about_ _the kids' safety_.

9.  _I understand. I'll dispatch a patrol car_ _to monitor the area_ _at those times_, | _and if we can pinpoint the driver_, | _we'll have a word with him_.
    我明白。我会在那个时段派巡逻警车去监控那个区域，| 如果我们能确认司机身份，| 我们会跟他谈谈的。

10. 谢谢警察同志。我们都希望他能明白这样做的后果，| 不要再超速了。| 我们想看到明显的改善。
    _Thank you, officer. We all hope_ _he can understand the consequences_ _of what he has done_ | _and can stop speeding_. | _We really want to see_ _some real improvements_.

11. _We'll do everything we can_ _to address this_. | _If you spot anything like this again_, | _please let us know immediately_.
    我们会尽一切努力来解决这个问题。| 如果您再次发现类似情况，| 请立即告诉我们。

12. 好的，我会继续关注的。| 希望这次投诉能起到作用。
    _Okay, I'll keep an eye out_. | _I hope this complaint_ _will make a difference_.

13. _Your report will definitely help_. | _We take traffic safety_ _very seriously_, | _especially in residential areas_.
    您的报告肯定会有帮助。| 我们非常重视交通安全，| 特别是在住宅区。

14. 谢谢您的帮助。| 我们都希望小区能更安全一些。

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two friends where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking house hunter. They are discussing property viewing and real estate opportunities. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there! Long time no see_! | _I had no clue_ _you are house hunting_!
    嘿！好久不见！| 我不知道你在看房呢。

2.  是呀。我们租房子住好多年了，| 我觉得，是时候买下一套属于自己的房子啦。
    _Exactly, we've been_ _renting for years_ | _and I feel it's time to_ _have a place of my own_.

3.  _I totally get it_. | _This area's super convenient_, | _with the mall and park nearby_. | _If you moved elsewhere_, _you'd have to_ _re-learn everything all over again_.
    我完全明白。| 这地段多方便啊，| 商场公园都在旁边。| 要是搬到别的地方，你就得重新熟悉一遍周边环境。

4.  可不是嘛，能不动地方最好了。| 我们不想让孩子们又要换学校，| 又要重新适应一遍周围的一切。
    _Absolutely, staying put would be ideal_. | _We don't want the kids_ _to have to switch schools_ | _and adjust to everything all over again_.

5.  _Exactly. The market is_ _flooded with listings now_, | _but it might take a bit_ _to find the right one_. | _Any luck so far_?
    确实，市面上现在房源很多，| 但找到合适的可能需要点时间。| 目前你有看中的吗？

6.  我们看了不少房子了，| 有一套房子我们特别中意，但是，价格超标了。| 我们不想让手头太紧。
    _We've seen quite a few properties_. | _There's one we really like_, _but it's over our budget_. | _We don't want to_ _stretch our finances_.

7.  _That's a shame_. | _But it's smart to_ _stick to your budget_. | _Don't worry, it doesn't mean_ _you won't find something you love_. | _There's plenty of fish in the sea_.
    真可惜，| 不过，量入为出是对的。| 别急，这不代表你们找不到喜欢的房子。| 好房子多的是。

8.  我们希望能买一套空房子，| 这样一切都简单。| 我不喜欢到处堆满家具和杂物的房子。| 我觉得我们没办法搬进那样的房子。
    _We'd like an empty property_ | _— that keeps things simple_. | _I don't like houses_ _cluttered with furniture and stuff_; | _I don't think we could_ _move into one like that_.

9.  _You may want to focus on_ _the floor plan_, | _rather than getting distracted by_ _the furnishings_. | _The decorations can always be changed later_.
    或许，你们可以关注房子的户型图，| 而不是被家具干扰。| 房子的装饰到后面都能改的。

10. 有些户型我们就是接受不了。| 我们不想要复式，| 只想要平层。
    _Some layouts_ _just won't work for us_; | _we don't want a two-story home_ | _—we prefer a single-level place_.

11. _It might be worth_ _checking out some of the older homes_ _in the area_. | _They often match_ _what you're looking for_. | _I can help you find them_.
    或许可以看看这个区一些年代久一些的房子 | ——它们往往更符合你们的需求。| 我可以帮你找找。

12. 谢谢你。我们不想大改结构。| 最多，微调一两个房间的布局，就可以啦。
    _Thank you. We don't want_ _major renovations_. | _At most, we'd just_ _tweak the layout_ _of one or two rooms_.

13. _Actually, there's one property_ _that could be perfect_, | _but it's not officially listed_. | _I know the owner personally_, | _and can set up an inspection_.
    其实，有一处房产可能很合适，| 但房子还没挂牌呢。| 我认识屋主，| 可以帮你们安排看房。

14. 太好了。帮我们安排一下吧。| 希望这次能成。| 真希望这套房子能满足我们全家的需求啊。
    _Fantastic! Please help arrange it for us_. | _I really hope this works out_! | _I really hope this house_ _will meet our family's needs_.

#70214. Customer Calls About Faulty Washer - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking appliance shop employee and a Mandarin-speaking customer. They are discussing a faulty washing machine and warranty service options. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there, this is_ _the appliance shop speaking_. | _My name is Adrian_. _How can I assist you_ today?
    你好，这里是电器商店。| 我是艾德利安。今天我能为您做点什么？

2.  你好！我前段时间在你们这里买了一台洗衣机，| 但最近坏掉了，| 总是发出尖锐的噪音，| 吓得我已经一周没用它了。
    _Hey there! I bought a washing machine_ _from you guys_ _a while back_, | _but it's been faulty lately_. | _It always makes a piercing noise_, | _and I've been too scared to use it_ _for a week_.

3.  _Oh no, sorry to hear that_. _Do you remember_ _exactly when you bought it_? | _If it's still under warranty_, | _we might be able to fix it_ _at no cost_.
    哎呀，听到这些我很抱歉。你还记得具体什么时候买吗？| 如果还在保修期内，| 我们可能可以免费维修。

4.  我是五个月前买的，之前一直运转得挺不错的，| 我原本还挺满意的。结果现在噪音又刺耳，又漏水。
    _I bought it five months ago_, _and it was working great_. | _I was actually pretty happy with it_. | _But now it's getting so noisy_ | _and it's even leaking water_.

5.  _That should still be covered_. | _Would you prefer getting it repaired_, | _or would you rather_ _we replace it for you_?
    这应该还在保修范围内。| 你希望我们修理它，| 还是换一台新的给你？

6.  是说我不用出钱修吗？| 我有点搞不清保修是什么意思。| 维修费用是不是都很高啊？
    _Does that mean I don't have to pay_? | _I'm not too sure_ _what warranty really means_. | _Is repair usually expensive_?

7.  _Exactly. Warranty means_ _we'll cover the repair_ _or even replace it for free_, | _as long as the issue_ _wasn't caused by misuse_.
    没错。保修就是在一定时间内，只要不是人为损坏，| 维修或更换都是免费的。

8.  太好了。我之前还担心得自己掏钱修。| 那我就放心了。| 我还是想把原机修好。
    _Great. I was worried_ _I'd have to pay out of pocket_. | _Then I'm relieved_. | _I'd prefer to_ _get the original machine fixed_.

9.  _Got it. I'll make sure_ _a technician gets out to you soon_. | _Can you tell me_ _when someone can come by_?
    明白了。我会安排技术员尽快过去。| 您什么时候方便让人上门看看？

10. 这个嘛，我做零售促销兼职，| 周一和周五不上班，| 这两天安排都可以。
    _Sure, I work part-time_ _in retail promotions_, | _and I'm off on Mondays and Fridays_. | _Either of those days_ _works for me_.

11. _That works. One of our technicians_ _will reach out_ _to set up an appointment_. | _The technician may need to run_ _a diagnostic cycle_ _to identify the fault_.
    好的。我们的技师会联系你预约具体时间。| 技师可能需要运行诊断程序来找出故障。

12. 这一套操作下来大概要多久？| 希望能快点修好。| 我在家等着的时候，要准备些什么吗？| 比如螺丝刀？
    _How long does_ _the whole process_ _usually take_? | _I really hope the washer_ _gets fixed soon_. | _When I'm waiting at home_, _should I_ _have anything ready_ | _—like a screwdriver_?

13. _The basic check usually takes_ _about half an hour_, | _and if we need to_ _open it up_ _for a motor inspection_, | _it will be around sixty minutes_. | _You don't have to_ _get any tools ready_.
    整套流程大概半小时，| 如果需要拆机检查电机，| 会大概 60 分钟。| 你不需要准备任何工具。

14. 好的，那我等你们联系我。| 希望这次能彻底修好，| 别再出问题了。
    _Okay, then I'll wait_ _for you to contact me_. | _I hope this time_ _it gets fixed properly_, | _and won't have any more problems_.

#70213. Strategies for School Band Fundraising - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking person and a Mandarin-speaking parent. They are discussing fundraising strategies for their school band program. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hey, come on in and_ _grab a chair_! | _My bad for being swamped yesterday_! | _Now I've got all the time_ _to chat about this_.
    嗨，快进来坐吧。| 昨天我太忙了实在不好意思，| 现在我时间很充裕，咱们慢慢聊。

2.  我之前是想跟你讨论，怎么给我们的学校乐队筹集资金，| 让孩子们有更多资金参加音乐巡演。| 你有什么想法吗？
    _I wanted to talk with you_ _about how to raise_ _some money for our school band_, | _so the kids can have_ _more funds to go on music tours_. | _Do you have any ideas_?

3.  _Well, I feel like_ _we could totally put together a fundraiser_. | _We just need to_ _pick the right kind of event_, | _like the kind of event_ _people would jump at attending_.
    嗯，我感觉咱们完全可以搞个筹款活动。| 我们只需要选对活动类型，| 需要大家迫不及待抢着来参加的那种活动。

4.  要不，我们弄一本附近商家的优惠券手册，| 卖给家长和社区居民？| 或者搞些附近商家的东西卖钱，怎么样？
    _How about this: we put together_ _a coupon book with deals_ _from the local businesses_, | _and sell it to parents_ _and people in the community_? | _Or maybe we could sell_ _some products from the local shops_ _to raise money_?

5.  _These are all great ideas_. | _But hey, how about_ _putting on a concert_ _for the school band_? | _We could use the school's_ _venue and equipment_, | _which would help_ _keep the costs down_.
    这些都很棒。| 不过哎，你觉得给学校乐队办场音乐会怎么样？| 我们可以用学校的场地和设施，| 这样可以节约开支。

6.  这主意靠谱！| 可以展现孩子们的才艺！| 家长们肯定乐意出钱支持的。| 我们多宣传，| 绝对人气爆棚！
    _That's a solid idea_! | _It'd be a great way_ _to show off_ _the kids' talents_. | _I'm sure the parents_ _would be more than happy_ _to chip in and support_. | _If we really get the word out_, | _people will definitely come_!

7.  _I think it's a solid idea too_! _Hosting the event_ _at school would save us_ _a lot on venue costs_. | _We could also invite_ _a few local bands_ _to come and perform_.
    我也觉得很好！在学校办活动，能省下大笔的场地费。| 我们还可以再请些本地乐队来表演助阵。

8.  我喜欢这个点子！| 还能让音乐会更专业，| 更热闹！| 乐队成员的亲友团绝对会来撑场子的！
    _I love that idea_! | _It would make_ | _the concert more_ | _professional and way_ | _more exciting_. | _The band members'_ | _friends and families_ | _are definitely gonna_ | _show up to support_!

9.  _Yeah, seeing these local bands_ _could really motivate the kids_ _to rehearse harder_. | _Plus, the local bands_ _might promote the concert_ _on their social media too_!
    是的，孩子们看到这些本地乐队，会更有动力排练。| 本地乐队也可能会在社交媒体宣传这次音乐会！

10. 太棒了，那就等于免费宣传了！| 我们可以再发动家长们制作蛋糕，甜点 | 和饮料来义卖。
    _Awesome, that basically means free promotion_! | _We could also get the parents_ _to make some cakes, desserts_, | _and drinks to sell_ _for fundraising_.

11. _Genius! That way_, _the vibe will be_ _way more enjoyable_! | _It would make the whole thing_ _more fun for everyone_!
    妙啊！这样现场气氛更愉快，| 每个人都能待得更开心！

12. 可以！细节方面，咱们得再敲定一下，| 还要联系附近商家，拉拉赞助。
    _Sounds good! We'll just need to_ _finalize the details_ | _and reach out to some local businesses_ _for sponsorship_.

13. _Absolutely! Shall we chat again_ _the day after tomorrow_? | _We'll also need to_ _apply early for permission_ _to use the school venue_.
    必须的！后天我们再碰一次怎么样？| 我们也需要早点跟学校申请场地使用的许可。

14. 好的，咱们到时候可以谈谈怎么分头 | 联系家长 | 和商家。| 我这几天先列个待办清单。
    _Alright. We can then_ _figure out how to_ _divide things up_— | _like who'll talk to the parents_ | _and who'll reach out to_ _the local businesses_. | _I'll put together_ _a to-do list_ _over the next few days_.

#70212. Newcomer Navigates Waste Sorting and Gardening - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking long-time resident and a Mandarin-speaking newcomer to the neighborhood. They are discussing waste sorting systems and local gardening practices. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi! We haven't had_ _a proper chat_ _since you moved here_! | _Found any good spots around here_?
    你好呀！自从你搬来，我们还没怎么好好聊过呢！| 发现附近有什么好地方了吗？

2.  你好。我暂时只摸清了超市和学校。| 不过，昨天我发现，这里的垃圾分类很不同。| 我正想找人问问呢。
    _Hi! So far, I've just figured out_ _the supermarket and the school_. | _But yesterday I noticed_ _the waste sorting system_ _here is quite different_. | _I was just wanting to ask someone_ _about it_.

3.  _Ah! The Aussie bin system_! | _That confuses everyone at first_. | _Tell me what's puzzling you_?
    啊！澳洲的垃圾桶系统啊！| 刚开始确实让人糊涂。| 跟我说说你哪里不明白呀？

4.  比如，为什么有三个不同颜色的垃圾桶？| 还有哪些垃圾要单独处理吗？
    _Like, why are there_ _three different colored bins_? | _And what waste needs_ _separate handling_?

5.  _Well, the red lid_ _is for general waste_, | _the yellow one_ _is for recycling_, | _and the green one_ _is for organics_. | _Some items, like batteries_, _need special drop-off_. | _Most supermarkets_ _take them_.
    嗯，红色盖子装普通垃圾，| 黄色回收，| 绿色有机垃圾。| 像电池这种特殊物品要单独处理。| 多数超市都有回收点。

6.  哦，所以，电池要单独处理呀。| 那么，旧的电子设备，我该扔到哪里呀？
    _Oh, so batteries_ _need separate handling_. | _Where should I dispose_ _of old electronic devices_ _then_?

7.  _The City Council holds_ _an e-waste collection day_ _quarterly_. | _The next one_ _will be in October_, | _at the community centre_.
    市政厅会每个季度办电子垃圾回收日，| 下次在十月，| 地点在社区中心。

8.  了解了。我还想种菜，| 我需要买几个高架菜床、| 一根浇水软管，| 还有其他园艺工具。| 你知道在哪里买吗？
    _Got it. I also want to_ _grow some vegetables_. | _I need to get_ _a few raised garden beds_, | _a watering hose_, | _and some other_ _gardening tools_. | _Do you know_ _where to buy them_?

9.  _I'd say, the gardening centre_ _along the highway_ _is your best bet_. | _It's quite big, and usually has_ _a wider range of stuff_.
    我觉得公路那边的园艺中心是你最好的选择。| 那地方挺大的，通常种类也更多。

10. 太好了。我搬家的时候啥园艺工具都没带过来。| 运费实在太贵了。| 所以现在我得重新添置一批。
    _Great. I didn't bring_ _any gardening tools_ _with me when I moved here_. | _The shipping costs_ _are too high_. | _So now I've got to_ _buy everything again_.

11. _I see. Picking out new tools_ _can actually be pretty fun_. | _Plus, that place_ _isn't too pricey_, | _which is a bonus_.
    我明白。其实挑新的工具也挺有意思的。| 而且那家店的价格不太贵，| 这算是个额外的好处。

12. 太好了。我已经迫不及待想种点东西了，| 就是这边的环境 | 跟我的祖国那边差很多。
    _Great. I really can't wait to_ _plant something_, | _it's just that the environment_ _here_ | _is so different_ _from back home_.

13. _How about I come with you_ _to the gardening centre now_? | _We can pick plants_ _that grow well_ _in our soil_.
    要不我现在陪你去园艺中心？| 我们可以选些适合本地土壤的植物。

14. 那太好了！我正担心选错植物呢。| 我们走吧，我开车，你可以坐副驾，给我指指路呀！
    _That'd be wonderful_! _I was just worried about_ _choosing the wrong plants_. | _Let's go. I'll drive, and you can_ _sit up front_ _and guide me_!

#70211. Puppy Course: Commands & Grooming - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking dog training center lead trainer and a Mandarin-speaking new puppy owner. They are discussing dog training courses, commands, and grooming services. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hey! I'm the lead trainer_ _at the Dog Training Center_. | _My coworker mentioned_ _you just adopted_ _an adorable male puppy_. | _What can I help you with_?
    你好！我是狗狗训练中心的首席训犬师。| 我同事说你刚领养了一只可爱的小公狗。| 我能帮你些什么？

2.  你好。是的，我刚领养了一只小狗。| 听说你们的小狗训练课程口碑很好，| 我想多了解一下。
    _Hi! Yeah, I just adopted_ _a puppy_. | _I heard your puppy training course_ _has a great reputation_. | _I'd love to learn more_.

3.  _Absolutely! We offer_ _a six-week course_ _here_ | _that covers basic commands_ _and hands-on handling techniques_.
    当然。我们这儿有个为期六周的课程，| 包括基本指令和实操训狗技巧。

4.  听起来很棒呀！我们家领养的小狗特别可爱的，| 很通人性，| 但也挺淘气。| 我想尽快让它开始上课。
    _That sounds great! The puppy we adopted_ _is super cute_. | _He is intuitive_, | _but he is also_ _quite naughty_. | _I'd love to get him started with_ _the course as soon as possible_.

5.  _That's a smart move_! | _Puppies are adorable_, | _and it's simpler_ _to nip unwanted habits_ _in the bud_. | _Our next session_ _starts in just a few days_.
    这个想法非常明智！| 小狗都很可爱，| 早点纠正坏习惯也会更容易。| 我们下期课几天后就开始了。

6.  那时间正好合适。| 我的孩子们经常跟小狗一起玩，| 所以我还想让孩子们一起参加，| 让他们也学学。
    _That's perfect timing_! | _My kids play with the puppy_ _all the time_, | _so I'd love for them_ _to join too_ | _—that way they can learn together_.

7.  _Absolutely! The class will teach_ _your kids_ _how to handle the puppy_, | _especially how to keep him_ _under control_ _during walks_.
    当然可以。课程会教你的孩子们控犬技巧，| 特别是遛狗时怎么控制小狗。

8.  太好啦！我的孩子们一个十岁，一个八岁，希望他们可以学习怎么照顾小狗，| 比如，怎么遛狗，怎么给小狗护理毛发，怎么科学喂养。
    _That's amazing! My kids are ten and eight_, _and I hope they could learn_ _how to take care of_ _the puppy_, | _you know, stuff like walking him_, _grooming him_, _and feeding him properly_.

9.  _Well, our course is_ _a perfect fit then_! | _The course also includes_ _socialization training_. | _We'll teach your pup_ _how to interact with_ _people and other animals_.
    嗯，那我们的课程就正合适啦。| 我们的课程还包社交训练，| 会教你家小狗怎么跟人和其他动物相处。

10. 太好啦。课程的价格是多少？| 课程会包含小狗笼养训练和上厕所训练吗？
    _That's great! How much_ _does the course cost_? | _And does it include_ _crate training and potty training_ _for the puppy_?

11. _Rest assured, the course covers everything_! | _You're in good hands_! | _It's 200 dollars for six weeks_. _By the way, is your pup_ _up to date_ _on all his shots_?
    放心吧，课程内容全包的。| 交给我们绝对靠谱的。| 课程价格是六周 200 澳币。对了，你的小狗疫苗打全了吗？

12. 课程价格挺合理的。| 下一期课我们能参加吗？小狗的疫苗都打过了。兽医给我疫苗证明了。
    _The price sounds very reasonable_. | _Can we join the next session_? | _The puppy's got all his shots_. | _The vet gave me_ _his vaccination certificate_.

13. _Perfect! Let's get_ _the little guy signed up now_. | _Don't forget his shot records_ _when you attend the first lesson_!
    太棒啦！咱们现在就给小家伙报名吧。| 第一堂课别忘了带好所有疫苗证明哟！

14. 太好啦。放心，我会带着的。希望能培养出一只听话不捣蛋的小狗！
    _Perfect! No worries, I'll bring them_. | _Hope we can raise a well-behaved_, _non-mischievous puppy_!

#70210. Making Use of a Spare Skip Bin - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two friends where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking business owner. They are discussing the use of a skip bin for waste disposal and offering mutual assistance. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hey, long time no see_! | _How are things shaping up_ _with your new business_?
    嘿，好久不见！你的新生意做得怎么样？

2.  你好呀！刚开始的几个月，真的挺辛苦的，| 不过，好在生意现在开始红火了，| 跟之前比，现在我忙多了。
    _Hey! The first few months_ _were really tough_, | _but gladly business_ _is getting busy now_. | _Compared to before_, _I'm way busier_ _these days_!

3.  _That's great news_. | _I've been told_ _the previous owner_ _of this building_ | _left a ton of junk here_ _when they left_.
    太好了。我听说这栋楼上一个房主搬走时，| 在这留下了一堆垃圾。

4.  确实，真让人头疼啊。| 我这阵子全心投入到生意里了，| 都没来得及顾这事呢。
    _Yeah, it's such a headache_. | _I've been so wrapped up_ _in the business_ | _that I haven't had a chance_ _to deal with it_.

5.  _Actually, I could lend a hand_. | _You probably saw_ _that I got a skip bin_ _delivered here last month_.
    实际上，我可以帮你一把。| 你可能看到了上个月我这送来一个大型垃圾箱。

6.  那么大的垃圾箱，我当然看到啦！| 你是打算用它清理仓库垃圾吗？你的垃圾肯定不少啊！
    _Of course I saw_ _that huge skip bin_! | _You're using it to clean out_ _the warehouse, right_? | _You must have a ton of junk_!

7.  _Funny enough, I don't_. | _It turned out much bigger_ _than I thought_. | _It's only half full_ _at the moment_. | _Do you need to use it_ _for your trash_?
    搞笑的是，我其实没多少垃圾。这箱子比我想象的大多了，| 现在才装了半箱。| 你要用这箱子扔你的垃圾吗？

8.  求之不得！谢谢你！我怀疑前一个业主压根没处理过垃圾，| 我能轻松就能把垃圾箱装满。
    _Perfect! Thank you_! | _I doubt the previous owner_ _never cleared the junk_. | _I could easily fill_ _this skip bin_!

9.  _Perfect! Make use of it_! | _It'd be a shame_ _to let it sit empty_. | _Hiring it costs a lot_!
    太好了！赶紧用起来！| 空着不用太浪费了。租这东西可不便宜啊！

10. 我知道租大垃圾箱有多贵，特别是租一周的话。| 你要我帮你分担一下费用吗？| 或者我可以给你的车提供一次保养，来感谢你给我用垃圾箱，| 这帮我省掉了大麻烦。
    _I know how expensive it is_ _to hire a skip bin_, _especially for a whole week_. | _Want me to chip in_? | _Or I could give your car a service_ _as a thank you_! | _—you just saved me_ _a ton of hassle_!

11. _I'd really appreciate_ _your generous offer_! | _Fantastic! My car is due for_ _a service anyway_, _so that's perfect_.
    感谢你这么大方！太好了！| 我车本来也该保养了，这下正好。

12. 非常乐意效劳！哪天你方便了，| 把钥匙给我就行。不会花太久时间的。
    _Happy to help_! | _Whenever it's convenient for you_, | _just give me the car key_. | _It won't take long_.

13. _Thanks. Just say the word_ _if you need a hand_ _hauling the junk_. | _I'll leave the skip bin here_ _till the weekend_.
    谢谢。如果需要帮忙搬垃圾，跟我说一声。| 我会把垃圾箱留到周末。

14. 真是太感谢你能帮忙了。如果你方便的话，| 我现在就可以开始清理。
    _I really appreciate your help_. | _If you've got time now_, | _I can start clearing out_ _right away_.

#70209. New Neighbour's Dog Barking - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two neighbours where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are discussing a new neighbour's dog that barks a lot and how to handle the situation. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there_! | _I'm your new neighbour_ _from next door_. | _I just moved in_ _last week_.
    你好！我是你隔壁的新邻居。我上周刚搬来。

2.  你好！欢迎来到这个社区！| 我是小明，很高兴认识你。
    _Hello! Welcome to the neighbourhood_! | _I'm Xiaoming_, _nice to meet you_.

3.  _Nice to meet you too_! | _I'm Sarah_. | _I hope I'm not bothering you_, | _but I wanted to ask_ _about the dog_ _that keeps barking_.
    很高兴认识你！我是莎拉。| 希望没有打扰到你，| 但我想问问那只一直叫的狗。

4.  哦，你说的是那只狗啊。| 它确实叫得挺厉害的，| 我也注意到了。
    _Oh, you mean that dog_. | _It does bark quite a lot_, | _I've noticed it too_.

5.  _It's been driving me crazy_ _since I moved in_. | _I can't get any sleep_ _at night_. | _Do you know_ _whose dog it is_?
    自从我搬来后，它就一直让我发疯。| 我晚上根本睡不着觉。| 你知道这是谁的狗吗？

6.  我知道，是新搬来的那家人养的。| 他们好像不太管那只狗，| 让它整天在外面叫。
    _I know, it belongs to_ _the new family that moved in_. | _They don't seem to care_ _about the dog much_, | _letting it bark outside all day_.

7.  _That's terrible_! | _I've tried talking to them_, | _but they don't seem to care_. | _What should I do_?
    太糟糕了！我试过跟他们谈，| 但他们似乎不在乎。| 我该怎么办？

8.  我建议你先去找社区委员会投诉。| 我们这里对噪音有严格规定，| 他们应该能帮你解决。
    _I suggest you first_ _complain to the community committee_. | _We have strict noise regulations here_, | _they should be able to help_.

9.  _That's a good idea_. | _I'll do that tomorrow_. | _In the meantime_, _do you have any suggestions_ _for dealing with the noise_?
    好主意。我明天就去。| 同时，你有什么建议| 来应对这个噪音吗？

10. 你可以试试戴耳塞睡觉，| 或者用白噪音机。| 我朋友用过，效果还不错。
    _You could try_ _wearing earplugs to sleep_, | _or use a white noise machine_. | _My friend used one_, _it worked quite well_.

11. _Thanks for the suggestions_! | _I'll definitely try_ _the earplugs tonight_. | _Hopefully the community committee_ _can help resolve this_.
    谢谢你的建议！我今晚肯定试试耳塞。| 希望社区委员会能帮助解决这个问题。

12. 不客气！如果还有其他问题，| 随时可以来找我。| 我们邻居之间应该互相帮助。
    _You're welcome_! _If you have other questions_, | _feel free to come to me anytime_. | _We neighbours should help each other_.

13. _That's very kind of you_. | _I really appreciate it_. | _Hopefully we can get this_ _dog situation sorted out soon_.
    你真是太好了。我真的很感激。| 希望我们很快就能解决这个狗的问题。

14. 一定会的！社区委员会办事效率很高。| 我们很快就能睡个好觉了。
    _Definitely! The community committee_ _works very efficiently_. | _We'll be able to sleep well_ _soon_.

#70208. Car Insurance Claim After Accident - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking insurance agent and a Mandarin-speaking customer who has been in a car accident and needs to make an insurance claim. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good morning, sir_. | _Thank you for calling_ _our insurance company_. | _How can I assist you today_?
    早上好，先生。感谢您致电我们保险公司。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好，我昨天发生了车祸，| 现在需要申请保险理赔。| 我的保单号是123456789。
    _Hello, I had a car accident yesterday_, | _and now I need to file_ _an insurance claim_. | _My policy number is 123456789_.

3.  _I'm sorry to hear_ _about your accident_. | _I hope you're okay_. | _Let me pull up_ _your policy details_ _first_.
    听到您发生车祸我很遗憾。希望您没事。让我先调出您的保单详情。

4.  谢谢关心，我没事，| 只是车子受损比较严重。| 对方司机承认了责任。
    _Thank you for your concern, I'm fine_, | _but the car is quite damaged_. | _The other driver admitted fault_.

5.  _That's good to hear_ _that you're okay_. | _I can see your policy_ _is active and comprehensive_. | _What happened_ _in the accident_?
    听到您没事很好。我可以看到您的保单是有效的综合险。事故中发生了什么？

6.  我在十字路口等红灯时，| 后面的车追尾了。| 我的车被撞得很严重，| 后保险杠完全变形了。
    _I was waiting at a red light_ _at an intersection_, | _when the car behind_ _rear-ended me_. | _My car was badly damaged_, | _the rear bumper_ _is completely deformed_.

7.  _I understand that_. | _Do you have_ _a police report_ _or any photos_ _of the damage_? | _This will help_ _with the claim process_.
    我明白了。您有警方报告或损坏的照片吗？这将有助于理赔流程。

8.  有的，我拍了照片，| 也有警方报告。| 报告编号是PR-2024-001。
    _Yes, I took photos_, | _and I have a police report_. | _The report number is PR-2024-001_.

9.  _Perfect. I'll need you to_ _email those photos_ _to claims@insurance.com_. | _Also, please provide_ _the other driver's details_.
    很好。我需要您把照片发到claims@insurance.com。另外，请提供对方司机的详细信息。

10. 好的，我马上发邮件。| 对方司机的信息我也有，| 包括姓名、电话和车牌号。
    _Okay, I'll send the email right away_. | _I also have_ _the other driver's information_, | _including name, phone, and license plate_.

11. _Excellent. Now, let me ask_ _a few more questions_. | _Was anyone else_ _in your car_ _at the time_?
    很好。现在让我再问几个问题。当时您车里还有其他人吗？

12. 没有，就我一个人。| 我系了安全带，| 所以没有受伤。
    _No, just me alone_. | _I was wearing a seatbelt_, | _so I wasn't injured_.

13. _That's very fortunate_. | _I'll start processing_ _your claim now_. | _You should receive_ _a claim number_ _within 24 hours_.
    那很幸运。我现在开始处理您的理赔。您应该在24小时内收到理赔号。

14. 太好了，谢谢你的帮助！| 还有什么需要我做的吗？
    _Great, thank you for your help_! | _Is there anything else_ _I need to do_?

15. _Just keep all receipts_ _for any expenses_ _related to the accident_. | _We'll reimburse you_ _for reasonable costs_. | _Thank you for choosing_ _our insurance company_.
    只要保留所有与事故相关的费用收据。我们会报销合理的费用。感谢您选择我们保险公司。

13. _Perfect, Mr. Li Ming_. | _I'll confirm your booking_ _for next Friday_ _at 7 PM_. | _You'll receive a confirmation email shortly_.
    很好，李先生。我会确认您下周五晚上7点的预订。您很快就会收到确认邮件。

    建议穿商务休闲装。如果您愿意，我们还可以安排生日蛋糕和装饰。

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking school principal and a Mandarin-speaking job candidate who is applying for a teaching position. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good morning_, _Ms. Chen_. | _Thank you for coming_ _to interview today_. | _I'm Principal Johnson_.

2.  早上好，约翰逊校长。| 很高兴见到您。| 感谢您给我这次面试机会。
    _Good morning_, _Principal Johnson_. | _Nice to meet you_. | _Thank you for giving me_ _this interview opportunity_.

3.  _You're welcome_. | _I've reviewed_ _your resume and qualifications_. | _You have an impressive background_ _in education_.
    不客气。我已经看过您的简历和资历了。您的教育背景令人印象深刻。

4.  谢谢您的认可。| 我在中国有8年的教学经验，| 主要教授英语和数学。
    _Thank you for your recognition_. | _I have 8 years_ _of teaching experience in China_, | _mainly teaching English and Mathematics_.

5.  _That's excellent. We're looking for_ _someone who can teach_ _both subjects_. | _What made you decide_ _to move to Australia_?
    这很好。我们正在寻找能教授这两门学科的人。是什么让您决定搬到澳大利亚的？

6.  我想体验不同的教育体系，| 学习新的教学方法。| 澳大利亚的教育理念很先进，| 我很想在这里发展。
    _I want to experience_ _different education systems_, | _and learn new teaching methods_. | _Australia's educational philosophy_ _is very advanced_, | _and I'd like to develop here_.

7.  _That's a great attitude_. | _How do you handle_ _students with different_ _learning abilities_ _in the same class_?
    这是很好的态度。您如何处理同一班级中学习能力不同的学生？

8.  我采用分层教学法，| 为不同水平的学生设计不同的任务。| 我还会组织小组活动，| 让能力强的学生帮助能力弱的学生。
    _I use differentiated instruction_, | _designing different tasks_ _for students at different levels_. | _I also organize group activities_, | _letting stronger students_ _help weaker ones_.

9.  _That's exactly_ _what we need here_. | _How do you communicate_ _with parents_ _about their children's progress_?
    这正是我们这里需要的。您如何与家长沟通他们孩子的进步情况？

10. 我定期与家长保持联系，| 通过电话、邮件或面谈。| 我会详细说明孩子的优点和需要改进的地方，| 并给出具体的建议。
    _I maintain regular contact_ _with parents_, | _through phone_, _email_, _or face-to-face meetings_. | _I'll explain in detail_ _the child's strengths_ _and areas for improvement_, | _and give specific suggestions_.

11. _Perfect. What would you do_ _if a student_ _was consistently disruptive_ _in your class_?
    很好。如果有学生在您的课堂上持续捣乱，您会怎么做？

12. 首先，我会私下与这个学生谈话，| 了解他为什么会有这种行为。| 然后制定一个行为改进计划，| 并与家长和学校辅导员合作。
    _First, I would talk privately_ _with this student_, | _to understand why_ _he behaves this way_. | _Then I would develop_ _a behavior improvement plan_, | _and work with parents_ _and school counselors_.

13. _That shows_ _good problem-solving skills_. | _One last question_: _when could you start_ _if we offer you_ _the position_?
    这显示了很好的解决问题的能力。最后一个问题：如果我们提供这个职位，您什么时候可以开始？

14. 我可以立即开始。| 我已经准备好了所有必要的文件，| 包括工作签证和教师资格证。
    _I can start immediately_. | _I have all the necessary documents ready_, | _including work visa_ _and teaching qualifications_.

15. _Excellent. I'll discuss this_ _with the school board_ _and get back to you_ _by the end of the week_. | _Thank you for your time_.
    很好。我会与学校董事会讨论这件事，并在本周末前回复您。感谢您的时间。

16. 谢谢您，约翰逊校长。| 我期待听到好消息。| 祝您有愉快的一天。
    _Thank you_, _Principal Johnson_. | _I look forward to_ _hearing good news_. | _Have a great day_.

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking car buyer and a Mandarin-speaking private car seller. They are discussing the purchase of a used car, including price negotiation and vehicle inspection. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there_! | _I saw your ad_ _for the 2018 Toyota Camry_. | _Is it still available_?
    你好！我看到了你2018年丰田凯美瑞的广告。还在卖吗？

2.  是的，还在卖。| 车况很好，| 只开了5万公里。| 你想看看车吗？
    _Yes, it's still for sale_. | _The car is in good condition_, | _only driven 50,000 km_. | _Do you want to see it_?

3.  _Absolutely! I'm looking for_ _a reliable family car_. | _Can you tell me_ _more about it_?
    当然！我正在找一辆可靠的家庭用车。你能告诉我更多关于它的信息吗？

4.  这辆车是我一手车，| 定期保养，| 没有出过事故。| 内饰也很干净。
    _This car is my first owner_, | _regularly maintained_, | _no accidents. The interior_ _is also clean_.

5.  _That sounds promising_. | _What's the asking price_? | _And are you flexible_ _on the price_?
    听起来不错。要价是多少？价格方面有商量余地吗？

6.  我标价是2万5千澳元，| 但如果你真心想买，| 我们可以谈谈。| 你觉得怎么样？
    _I'm asking for $25,000_, | _but if you're really interested_, | _we can negotiate_. | _What do you think_?

7.  _That's a bit higher_ _than I expected_. | _I've seen similar cars_ _for around $22,000_. | _Could you come down_ _to that price_?
    比我预期的要高一些。我见过类似的车型大约2万2千澳元。你能降到那个价格吗？

8.  2万2千有点低了，| 但如果你今天能定下来，| 我可以考虑2万3千。| 这个价格很合理了。

10. 当然可以。| 你有驾照吗？| 我们可以开一圈，| 大概15分钟。
    _Of course. Do you have_ _a driver's license_? | _We can take a drive around_, | _about 15 minutes_.

11. _Perfect. I have my license_. | _Let's go for_ _a test drive_. | _I want to check_ _the engine_, _brakes_, _and transmission_.
    很好。我有驾照。我们去试驾吧。我想检查发动机、刹车和变速箱。

12. 没问题。| 车就在那边，| 钥匙给你。| 你可以仔细检查。
    _No problem. The car_ _is over there_, | _here are the keys_. | _You can check carefully_.

13. _Thanks. The car drives well_. | _But I noticed_ _the air conditioning_ _isn't working properly_. | _That's a concern_.
    谢谢。车开起来不错。但我注意到空调工作不正常。这让我担心。

14. 空调确实有点问题，| 但修起来不贵，| 大概200澳元就能修好。| 我可以再降500澳元。
    _The air conditioning_ _does have some issues_, | _but it's not expensive to fix_, | _about $200. I can reduce_ _another $500_.

15. _That's fair. So the final price_ _would be $22,500_? | _And you'll include_ _the service history_ _and registration papers_?
    这很公平。所以最终价格是2万2千5百澳元？你还会包括维修历史和注册文件吗？

16. 是的，所有文件都包括。| 如果你同意这个价格，| 我们可以今天完成交易。| 现金或银行转账都可以。
    _Yes, all documents included_. | _If you agree to this price_, | _we can complete the transaction today_. | _Cash or bank transfer_ _are both fine_.

17. _Great! I'll take it_ _for $22,500_. | _Let's go inside_ _and complete_ _the paperwork_.
    很好！我以2万2千5百澳元买下它。我们进去完成文件手续吧。

#70204. Reporting a Lost Credit Card - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking bank customer service representative and a Mandarin-speaking customer who has lost their credit card and needs to report it immediately. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good morning_, _welcome to_ _First National Bank_. | _How may I assist you today_?
    早上好，欢迎光临第一国民银行。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好，我的信用卡丢了，| 我需要立即挂失。| 我很担心有人会盗用我的卡。
    _Hello, I lost my credit card_, | _and I need to report it_ _immediately_. | _I'm worried someone_ _might use it fraudulently_.

3.  _I understand_ _your concern_. | _Let me help you_ _report this right away_. | _What's your account number_?
    我理解您的担心。让我立即帮您挂失。您的账号是多少？

4.  我的账号是1234-5678-9012-3456。| 我的名字是张伟，| 身份证号是123456789012345678。
    _My account number_ _is 1234-5678-9012-3456_. | _My name is Zhang Wei_, | _and my ID number_ _is 123456789012345678_.

5.  _Thank you_, _Mr. Zhang_. | _I can see your account_. | _When did you last see_ _your credit card_?
    谢谢您，张先生。我可以看到您的账户。您最后一次看到信用卡是什么时候？

6.  昨天下午3点左右，| 我在购物中心购物时还在用。| 回家后发现钱包不见了，| 信用卡就在钱包里。
    _Yesterday around 3 PM_, | _I was still using it_ _at the shopping mall_. | _When I got home_, _I found my wallet missing_, | _and the credit card_ _was in the wallet_.

7.  _I'll cancel your card_ _immediately_. | _This will prevent_ _any unauthorized transactions_. | _Do you want me to_ _order a replacement card_?
    我会立即取消您的卡。这将防止任何未经授权的交易。您要我为您订购一张新卡吗？

8.  是的，请帮我订一张新卡。| 新卡什么时候能到？| 我需要支付什么费用吗？
    _Yes, please order_ _a new card for me_. | _When will the new card arrive_? | _Do I need to pay_ _any fees_?

9.  _The replacement card_ _will arrive_ _in 5-7 business days_. | _There's a $15 fee_ _for the replacement_, | _but I can waive it_ _this time_.
    新卡将在5-7个工作日内到达。换卡需要15美元的费用，但我这次可以为您免除。

10. 太好了，谢谢您！| 新卡到了之后，| 我需要激活它吗？
    _Great, thank you_! | _After the new card arrives_, | _do I need to activate it_?

11. _Yes, you'll need to_ _activate it_ _by calling our hotline_ _or using our mobile app_. | _The activation instructions_ _will come with the card_.
    是的，您需要通过拨打我们的热线或使用我们的手机应用来激活它。激活说明会随卡一起寄来。

12. 好的，我明白了。| 现在我的旧卡已经完全不能用了，对吗？
    _Okay, I understand_. | _Now my old card_ _is completely unusable_, _right_?

13. _Correct. The old card_ _has been cancelled_ _and cannot be used_ _for any transactions_. | _If you find it later_, _please destroy it_.
    正确。旧卡已经被取消，不能用于任何交易。如果您后来找到了它，请销毁它。

14. 明白了。还有什么其他需要注意的吗？| 比如监控我的账户活动？
    _I understand_. | _Is there anything else_ _I should know_? | _Like monitoring_ _my account activity_?

15. _Yes, please monitor_ _your account regularly_ _for any suspicious transactions_. | _We'll also send you_ _alerts for any unusual activity_.
    是的，请定期监控您的账户，查看是否有可疑交易。我们也会为任何异常活动发送警报。

16. 好的，我会密切关注。| 谢谢您的帮助，| 我现在感觉安心多了。
    _Okay, I'll keep a close eye_. | _Thank you for your help_, | _I feel much more at ease now_.

17. _You're welcome_, _Mr. Zhang_. | _Is there anything else_ _I can help you with today_?
    不客气，张先生。今天还有其他我可以帮助您的吗？

18. 没有了，谢谢您。| 祝您有愉快的一天。
    _No, that's all, thank you_. | _Have a great day_.

---

#70203. Applying for a Library Card - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking library staff member and a Mandarin-speaking person who wants to apply for a library card. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good afternoon_, _welcome to_ _Central Library_. | _How may I help you today_?
    下午好，欢迎光临中央图书馆。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好，我想申请一张借书证。| 我是新来的移民，| 想在这里借书学习英语。
    _Hello, I'd like to apply_ _for a library card_. | _I'm a new immigrant_, | _and I want to borrow books_ _to learn English_.

3.  _That's wonderful! We have a great collection_ _of English learning materials_. | _Let me help you_ _with the application_.
    这很好！我们有很棒的英语学习材料收藏。让我帮您办理申请。

4.  太好了！我需要带什么证件吗？| 我有护照和地址证明。
    _Great! What documents_ _do I need to bring_? | _I have my passport_ _and proof of address_.

5.  _Perfect! I'll need to see_ _both of those_. | _Can you also provide_ _a phone number_ _and email address_?
    很好！我需要看这两个证件。您还能提供电话号码和电子邮件地址吗？

6.  当然可以。| 我的电话是0412-345-678，| 邮箱是zhang.wei@email.com。
    _Of course. My phone number_ _is 0412-345-678_, | _and my email_ _is zhang.wei@email.com_.

7.  _Excellent. Now let me ask_ _a few questions_. | _What type of books_ _are you most interested in_?
    很好。现在让我问几个问题。您对什么类型的书最感兴趣？

8.  我想看一些简单的英语小说，| 还有英语学习教材。| 我刚开始学英语，| 所以需要初级水平的书。
    _I want to read_ _some simple English novels_, | _and English learning textbooks_. | _I'm just starting_ _to learn English_, | _so I need beginner-level books_.

9.  _That's perfect! We have a special section_ _for English learners_. | _You can borrow up to_ _10 books at once_.
    这很好！我们有专门的英语学习者区域。您一次可以借10本书。

10. 10本书？太好了！| 借书期限是多久？| 如果逾期了会有什么后果？
    _10 books? That's great_! | _How long_ _can I keep them_? | _What happens_ _if I return them late_?

11. _Books can be borrowed_ _for 3 weeks_. | _You can renew them_ _for another 3 weeks_ _if no one else_ _has requested them_.
    书可以借3周。如果没有其他人预约，您可以再续借3周。

12. 续借？怎么操作？| 可以在网上续借吗？
    _Renew? How does that work_? | _Can I renew online_?

13. _Yes, absolutely! You can renew online_ _using your library card number_ _and PIN_. | _Or you can call us_ _or visit in person_.
    是的，当然可以！您可以使用借书证号码和PIN在网上续借。或者您可以打电话给我们或亲自来访。

14. 明白了。还有什么其他服务吗？| 比如电脑使用或打印？
    _I understand. Are there other services_? | _Like computer use_ _or printing_?

15. _Yes, we offer_ _free computer access_ _and internet_. | _Printing costs_ _10 cents per page_. | _You can also access_ _our online resources_.
    是的，我们提供免费的电脑使用和互联网。打印每页10美分。您还可以访问我们的在线资源。

16. 在线资源？都有什么？
    _Online resources? What are they_?

17. _We have e-books_, _audiobooks_, _language learning apps_, | _and online courses_. | _All free with your library card_.
    我们有电子书、有声书、语言学习应用和在线课程。有了借书证，这些都是免费的。

18. 太棒了！| 我现在就可以拿到借书证吗？
    _That's amazing! Can I get_ _my library card now_?

19. _Yes, I'll process it_ _right away_. | _Here's your card_ _and PIN_. | _You can start borrowing_ _books immediately_.
    是的，我立即为您办理。这是您的卡和PIN。您可以立即开始借书。

20. 谢谢您！| 我现在就可以去选书了吗？
    _Thank you! Can I go_ _choose books now_?

21. _Absolutely! The English learning section_ _is on the second floor_. | _If you need help_, _just ask_ _any staff member_.
    当然可以！英语学习区域在二楼。如果您需要帮助，就问任何工作人员。

#70202. Ordering Takeaway Food - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking restaurant staff member and a Mandarin-speaking customer who wants to order takeaway food. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good evening_, _welcome to_ _Golden Wok Restaurant_. | _How may I help you today_?
    晚上好，欢迎光临金锅餐厅。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好，我想订外卖。| 你们现在还在营业吗？
    _Hello, I'd like to order takeaway_. | _Are you still open now_?

3.  _Yes, we're open_ _until 10 PM_. | _What would you like_ _to order today_?
    是的，我们营业到晚上10点。您今天想点什么？

4.  我想点一份宫保鸡丁，| 一份麻婆豆腐，| 还有一份蛋炒饭。| 这些菜辣吗？
    _I'd like to order_ _Kung Pao Chicken_, | _Mapo Tofu_, | _and Egg Fried Rice_. | _Are these dishes spicy_?

5.  _The Kung Pao Chicken_ _is moderately spicy_, | _and the Mapo Tofu_ _is quite spicy_. | _The Egg Fried Rice_ _is not spicy at all_.
    宫保鸡丁是中等辣度，麻婆豆腐比较辣。蛋炒饭一点都不辣。

6.  好的，那宫保鸡丁和麻婆豆腐都少放点辣椒。| 大概需要多长时间？
    _Okay, then please put less chili_ _in the Kung Pao Chicken_ _and Mapo Tofu_. | _How long_ _will it take_?

7.  _It will take_ _about 20-25 minutes_. | _Would you like to_ _wait here_ _or come back later_?
    大约需要20-25分钟。您想在这里等还是稍后再来？

8.  我在这里等吧。| 总共多少钱？
    _I'll wait here_. | _How much is the total_?

9.  _Let me calculate_: | _Kung Pao Chicken is $18_, | _Mapo Tofu is $16_, | _and Egg Fried Rice is $12_. | _Total is $46_.
    让我计算一下：宫保鸡丁18美元，麻婆豆腐16美元，蛋炒饭12美元。总共46美元。

10. 好的，我付现金。| 你们接受信用卡吗？
    _Okay, I'll pay in cash_. | _Do you accept credit cards_?

11. _Yes, we accept_ _both cash and credit cards_. | _We also accept_ _mobile payments_ _like Apple Pay_.
    是的，我们接受现金和信用卡。我们也接受移动支付，比如Apple Pay。

12. 那我用信用卡付吧。| 这是我的卡。
    _Then I'll pay_ _with credit card_. | _Here's my card_.

13. _Thank you. Your total is $46_. | _Please insert your card_ _or tap it_.
    谢谢您。您的总额是46美元。请插入您的卡或轻触它。

14. 好的，我轻触一下。
    _Okay, I'll tap it_.

15. _Perfect. Your payment_ _has been processed_. | _Your order number_ _is 1234_. | _Please wait_ _for your food_.
    很好。您的付款已经处理完成。您的订单号是1234。请等待您的食物。

16. 谢谢！| 我可以在那边坐着等吗？
    _Thank you! Can I sit_ _over there to wait_?

17. _Of course! There are some chairs_ _by the window_. | _We'll call your number_ _when it's ready_.
    当然可以！窗边有一些椅子。准备好时我们会叫您的号码。

18. 太好了！| 谢谢您的帮助。
    _Great! Thank you for your help_.

#70201. Asking for Directions to Tourist Attractions - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking local resident and a Mandarin-speaking tourist who is asking for directions to popular tourist attractions in the city. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Excuse me_, _sir_. | _I'm a tourist_ _and I'm a bit lost_. | _Can you help me_ _find my way_?
    打扰一下，先生。我是游客，有点迷路了。您能帮我找到路吗？

2.  当然可以！| 我很乐意帮助游客。| 您想去哪里？
    _Of course! I'm happy to help tourists_. | _Where do you want to go_?

3.  _I want to visit_ _the famous Opera House_. | _I heard it's_ _a must-see attraction_. | _How do I get there_?
    我想参观著名的歌剧院。我听说这是必看的景点。我怎么去那里？

4.  歌剧院确实很棒！| 从这里走路大约需要20分钟，| 或者您可以坐公交车。
    _The Opera House_ _is indeed amazing_! | _It's about 20 minutes_ _walk from here_, | _or you can take a bus_.

5.  _I prefer walking_ _to see the city_. | _Can you give me_ _simple directions_?
    我更喜欢走路看城市。您能给我简单的指示吗？

6.  好的，很简单。| 沿着这条街一直走，| 到第三个路口右转，| 然后一直走到海边。
    _Sure, it's simple_. | _Go straight along this street_, | _turn right at the third intersection_, | _then keep going_ _until you reach the waterfront_.

7.  _That sounds easy enough_. | _What about_ _the Harbour Bridge_? | _Is it close_ _to the Opera House_?
    听起来很简单。海港大桥呢？它离歌剧院近吗？

8.  是的，很近！| 从歌剧院步行到海港大桥只需要10分钟。| 两个景点可以一起参观。
    _Yes, very close_! | _It's only 10 minutes_ _walk from the Opera House_ _to the Harbour Bridge_. | _You can visit both attractions together_.

9.  _Perfect! Are there any_ _good restaurants nearby_? | _I'd like to try_ _local food_.
    很好！附近有什么好餐厅吗？我想尝尝当地美食。

10. 当然有！| 在歌剧院附近有很多餐厅，| 特别是海鲜餐厅。| 我推荐"悉尼海鲜"。
    _Of course! There are many restaurants_ _near the Opera House_, | _especially seafood restaurants_. | _I recommend "Sydney Seafood"_.

11. _That sounds delicious_! | _What about shopping areas_? | _I want to buy_ _some souvenirs_.
    听起来很美味！购物区呢？我想买一些纪念品。

12. 在歌剧院附近有"岩石区"，| 那里有很多纪念品商店和手工艺品店。| 价格也比较合理。
    _Near the Opera House_ _there's "The Rocks"_, | _with many souvenir shops_ _and craft stores_. | _The prices are also reasonable_.

13. _Great! How long should I plan_ _to spend_ _at these attractions_?
    很好！我应该计划在这些景点花多长时间？

14. 建议您至少安排半天时间。| 歌剧院参观需要1-2小时，| 海港大桥拍照30分钟，| 岩石区购物1-2小时。
    _I recommend_ _at least half a day_. | _Opera House tour_ _takes 1-2 hours_, | _Harbour Bridge photos_ _30 minutes_, | _The Rocks shopping_ _1-2 hours_.

15. _Thank you so much_ _for your help_! | _You've been very helpful_.
    非常感谢您的帮助！您帮了我很多。

16. 不客气！| 祝您在悉尼玩得开心！| 如果还有问题，随时可以问我。
    _You're welcome! Have a great time_ _in Sydney_! | _If you have more questions_, _feel free to ask me anytime_.

#70200. Discussing Weather and Seasonal Activities - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two friends where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are discussing the weather and planning seasonal activities together. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there_! | _How's the weather_ _in your area today_? | _It's been raining_ _all morning here_.
    你好！你们那边今天天气怎么样？我们这里整个上午都在下雨。

2.  我们这里天气很好！| 阳光明媚，温度适中。| 很适合户外活动。
    _The weather here is great_! | _Sunny and mild temperature_. | _Perfect for outdoor activities_.

3.  _That sounds wonderful_! | _I'm jealous. The rain has been_ _so heavy lately_. | _I can't wait_ _for summer_.
    听起来很棒！我很羡慕。最近雨下得很大。我等不及夏天了。

4.  夏天确实很棒！| 我们可以去海滩游泳，| 或者去公园野餐。| 你有什么计划吗？
    _Summer is indeed great_! | _We can go swimming_ _at the beach_, | _or have a picnic_ _in the park_. | _What are your plans_?

5.  _I'm thinking of_ _going camping_ _in the mountains_. | _The weather should be_ _perfect for hiking_. | _Would you like to join_?
    我在考虑去山里露营。天气应该很适合徒步旅行。你想加入吗？

6.  露营听起来很有趣！| 我从来没去过，| 需要准备什么装备吗？
    _Camping sounds fun_! | _I've never been before_, | _what equipment_ _do we need to prepare_?

7.  _We'll need tents_, _sleeping bags_, _and camping gear_. | _I have most of it_, | _so you don't need_ _to worry_.
    我们需要帐篷、睡袋和露营装备。我大部分都有，所以你不用担心。

8.  太好了！| 我们什么时候去？| 需要提前预订露营地吗？
    _Great! When are we going_? | _Do we need to book_ _a campsite in advance_?

9.  _Yes, we should book_ _at least a week ahead_. | _I'm thinking next month_. | _The weather should be_ _perfect then_.
    是的，我们应该至少提前一周预订。我在想下个月。那时天气应该很好。

10. 下个月很好！| 我可以请假。| 我们会在那里待几天？
    _Next month is perfect_! | _I can take time off_. | _How many days_ _will we stay there_?

11. _I'm thinking_ _3 days and 2 nights_. | _That gives us_ _plenty of time_ _to explore_ _and relax_.
    我在想3天2夜。这样我们有足够的时间探索和放松。

12. 听起来很棒！| 我们还可以看星星，| 听说山里的夜空很美。
    _Sounds great! We can also_ _look at the stars_, | _I heard the night sky_ _in the mountains is beautiful_.

13. _Absolutely! The stars are amazing_ _in the mountains_. | _We should also bring_ _a camera_ _to capture_ _the beautiful scenery_.
    当然！山里的星星很神奇。我们还应该带相机来捕捉美丽的风景。

14. 好主意！| 我负责带相机和零食。| 你负责帐篷和装备。
    _Good idea! I'll bring the camera_ _and snacks_. | _You're responsible for_ _tents and equipment_.

15. _Perfect! This is going to be_ _an amazing trip_. | _I can't wait_ _to show you_ _the beautiful mountain views_.
    完美！这将是一次很棒的旅行。我等不及要向你展示美丽的山景了。

16. 我也很期待！| 这将是我第一次露营经历，| 我相信会很难忘。
    _I'm also looking forward to it_! | _This will be my first_ _camping experience_, | _I believe it will be unforgettable_.

#70199. Booking a Doctor's Appointment - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking medical receptionist and a Mandarin-speaking patient who wants to book an appointment with a doctor. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good morning_, _welcome to_ _City Medical Centre_. | _How may I help you today_?
    早上好，欢迎光临城市医疗中心。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好，我想预约看医生。| 我最近感觉不太舒服。
    _Hello, I'd like to book_ _an appointment with a doctor_. | _I haven't been feeling well_ _lately_.

3.  _I'm sorry to hear_ _that you're not feeling well_. | _What symptoms_ _are you experiencing_?
    听到您感觉不舒服我很遗憾。您有什么症状？

4.  我最近总是头痛，| 而且感觉很疲劳。| 我想做个全面检查。
    _I've been having headaches_ _recently_, | _and feeling very tired_. | _I'd like to have_ _a comprehensive check-up_.

5.  _I understand. We have several doctors_ _available this week_. | _Do you have_ _a preference_ _for a specific doctor_?
    我明白了。我们这周有几位医生可用。您有特定的医生偏好吗？

6.  没有特别的偏好，| 但我希望是女医生。| 这样我会感觉更自在一些。
    _No particular preference_, | _but I hope it's a female doctor_. | _I'd feel more comfortable_ _that way_.

7.  _Of course. Dr. Sarah Johnson_ _has availability_ _on Thursday afternoon_. | _Would 2 PM_ _work for you_?
    当然可以。莎拉·约翰逊医生周四下午有空。下午2点对您来说可以吗？

8.  周四下午2点很好。| 我需要提前多久到？
    _Thursday 2 PM is perfect_. | _How early do I need_ _to arrive_?

9.  _Please arrive_ _15 minutes early_ _to fill out_ _the necessary forms_. | _Do you have_ _your Medicare card_?
    请提前15分钟到达，填写必要的表格。您有Medicare卡吗？

10. 有的，我带了。| 我还需要带什么其他证件吗？
    _Yes, I have it_. | _Do I need to bring_ _any other documents_?

11. _Just bring_ _your Medicare card_ _and a form of ID_. | _If you have_ _a list of medications_, _that would be helpful too_.
    只需要带您的Medicare卡和身份证。如果您有药物清单，那也会很有帮助。

12. 好的，我会准备的。| 这次预约大概需要多长时间？
    _Okay, I'll prepare them_. | _How long will this appointment take_?

13. _The initial consultation_ _usually takes_ _about 30 minutes_. | _If you need tests_, _that might take longer_.
    初次咨询通常需要30分钟左右。如果您需要做检查，可能需要更长时间。

14. 明白了。| 如果我想取消或改期，| 需要提前多久通知？
    _I understand. If I want_ _to cancel or reschedule_, | _how much notice_ _do I need to give_?

15. _We require_ _24 hours notice_ _for cancellations_. | _You can call us_ _or use our online system_.
    我们要求取消预约提前24小时通知。您可以打电话给我们或使用我们的在线系统。

16. 好的，我记住了。| 还有什么其他需要注意的吗？
    _Okay, I'll remember that_. | _Is there anything else_ _I should know_?

17. _That's all for now_. | _Your appointment_ _is confirmed for Thursday_ _at 2 PM_. | _We'll send you_ _a reminder_ _the day before_.
    现在就是这些了。您的预约确认在周四下午2点。我们会在前一天发送提醒。

18. 太好了！| 谢谢您的帮助。| 周四见！
    _Great! Thank you for your help_. | _See you Thursday_!

#70198. Discussing Hobbies and Interests - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two friends where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are discussing their hobbies and interests, sharing what they enjoy doing in their free time. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there_! | _What do you like_ _to do_ _in your free time_? | _I'm always curious_ _about people's hobbies_.
    你好！你在空闲时间喜欢做什么？我总是对人们的爱好很好奇。

2.  我喜欢很多活动！| 我最喜欢的是摄影，| 特别是风景摄影。| 你呢？
    _I like many activities_! | _My favorite is photography_, | _especially landscape photography_. | _What about you_?

3.  _That's interesting_! | _I love photography too_. | _What kind of camera_ _do you use_? | _I have a DSLR_.
    很有趣！我也喜欢摄影。你用什么相机？我有一台单反相机。

4.  我有一台索尼微单相机，| 虽然不是最贵的，| 但拍出来的照片质量很好。| 你主要拍什么？
    _I have a Sony mirrorless camera_, | _though not the most expensive_, | _but the photo quality is very good_. | _What do you mainly photograph_?

5.  _I mostly take_ _street photography_ _and portraits_. | _I find people_ _very interesting subjects_. | _What about landscapes_ _do you enjoy_?
    我主要拍街头摄影和人像。我觉得人是非常有趣的主题。你喜欢什么样的风景？

6.  我喜欢拍自然风景，| 特别是日出和日落。| 我还喜欢拍城市建筑，| 特别是古老的建筑。
    _I like photographing_ _natural landscapes_, | _especially sunrises and sunsets_. | _I also like photographing_ _city buildings_, | _especially old architecture_.

7.  _That sounds beautiful_! | _Do you also enjoy_ _other creative hobbies_? | _I love painting_ _and drawing_.
    听起来很美！你还喜欢其他创意爱好吗？我喜欢绘画和素描。

8.  绘画？太棒了！| 我从来没学过，| 但我很羡慕会画画的人。| 你画什么风格？
    _Painting? That's amazing_! | _I've never learned_, | _but I admire people_ _who can paint_. | _What style_ _do you paint_?

9.  _I mostly do_ _watercolor landscapes_ _and abstract art_. | _It's very relaxing_. | _Would you like_ _to try painting_ _sometime_?
    我主要画水彩风景和抽象艺术。这很放松。你想什么时候试试绘画吗？

10. 我很想试试！| 但我担心画不好。| 你有什么建议给初学者吗？
    _I'd love to try_! | _But I'm worried_ _I won't paint well_. | _Do you have any advice_ _for beginners_?

11. _Don't worry_ _about being perfect_! | _Just start with_ _simple shapes_ _and have fun_. | _Everyone starts_ _as a beginner_.
    不要担心完美！从简单的形状开始，享受乐趣。每个人都是从初学者开始的。

12. 你说得对！| 我决定试试。| 除了摄影和绘画，| 你还喜欢什么其他活动？
    _You're right! I've decided to try_. | _Besides photography and painting_, | _what other activities_ _do you enjoy_?

13. _I love hiking_ _and camping_ _in nature_. | _Being outdoors_ _helps me relax_. | _Do you enjoy_ _outdoor activities too_?
    我喜欢在大自然中徒步旅行和露营。户外活动帮助我放松。你也喜欢户外活动吗？

14. 是的！| 我喜欢徒步旅行，| 特别是爬山。| 我还喜欢游泳和骑自行车。
    _Yes! I like hiking_, | _especially mountain climbing_. | _I also like swimming_ _and cycling_.

15. _That's great! We have_ _so many interests_ _in common_. | _Maybe we could_ _go hiking together_ _sometime_.
    这很好！我们有这么多共同的兴趣。也许我们可以什么时候一起去徒步旅行。

16. 好主意！| 我知道附近有一些很好的徒步路线。| 我们可以计划一次周末旅行。
    _Great idea! I know some good_ _hiking trails nearby_. | _We can plan_ _a weekend trip_.

17. _Perfect! It's wonderful_ _to find someone_ _who shares_ _similar interests_. | _We'll have_ _a great time together_.
    完美！找到有相似兴趣的人真是太好了。我们在一起会很开心。

18. 我完全同意！| 有共同爱好的朋友让生活更有趣。| 我很期待我们的徒步旅行！
    _I completely agree_! | _Friends with common hobbies_ _make life more interesting_. | _I'm looking forward to_ _our hiking trip_!

#70197. Renting an Apartment - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking real estate agent and a Mandarin-speaking person who wants to rent an apartment. They are discussing available properties, requirements, and rental terms. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good morning_, _welcome to_ _City Real Estate_. | _How may I help you today_?
    早上好，欢迎光临城市房地产。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好，我想租一套公寓。| 我刚刚搬到这个城市，| 需要找个地方住。
    _Hello, I'd like to rent an apartment_. | _I just moved to this city_, | _and need a place to live_.

3.  _Welcome to the city_! | _I'd be happy_ _to help you_ _find a place_. | _What are you looking for_?
    欢迎来到这个城市！我很乐意帮您找地方。您在找什么样的？

4.  我想要一套两居室的公寓，| 最好在市中心附近，| 交通要方便。| 预算大概每月2000澳元。
    _I want a two-bedroom apartment_, | _preferably near the city center_, | _with convenient transportation_. | _Budget is about $2000 per month_.

5.  _That's a good budget_. | _I have several options_ _that might suit you_. | _Do you have_ _any specific requirements_?
    这是个不错的预算。我有几个可能适合您的选择。您有什么具体要求吗？

6.  我希望有停车位，| 最好有阳台，| 而且要有基本的家具。| 你们有带家具的公寓吗？
    _I hope to have parking_, | _preferably with a balcony_, | _and basic furniture_. | _Do you have furnished apartments_?

7.  _Yes, we do have_ _some furnished options_. | _Let me show you_ _a few properties_. | _This one has_ _2 bedrooms_, _parking_, _and a balcony_.
    是的，我们确实有一些带家具的选择。让我给您看几个房产。这个有2个卧室、停车位和阳台。

8.  听起来不错！| 这个公寓在哪里？| 离地铁站近吗？
    _Sounds good! Where is this apartment_? | _Is it close_ _to the subway station_?

9.  _It's located_ _in the downtown area_, | _just 5 minutes walk_ _from the central station_. | _There are also_ _many shops and restaurants nearby_.
    它位于市中心区域，距离中央车站步行只需5分钟。附近还有很多商店和餐厅。

10. 太好了！| 这个公寓有多大？| 月租是多少？
    _Great! How big is this apartment_? | _What's the monthly rent_?

11. _It's 85 square meters_ _with 2 bedrooms_, _1 bathroom_, _and a kitchen_. | _The monthly rent_ _is $1,800_, _plus utilities_.
    85平方米，有2个卧室、1个浴室和厨房。月租是1800澳元，加上水电费。

12. 水电费大概多少钱？| 我需要付押金吗？
    _How much are utilities approximately_? | _Do I need to pay_ _a deposit_?

13. _Utilities are usually_ _around $150-200 per month_. | _Yes, we require_ _a security deposit_ _of one month's rent_.
    水电费通常是每月150-200澳元。是的，我们需要一个月的租金作为押金。

14. 明白了。| 我可以先看看房子吗？| 什么时候方便？
    _I understand. Can I see_ _the apartment first_? | _When is convenient_?

15. _Of course! I can show you_ _tomorrow afternoon_ _at 2 PM_. | _Does that time_ _work for you_?
    当然可以！我可以在明天下午2点带您看房。那个时间对您来说可以吗？

16. 明天下午2点很好！| 我需要带什么证件吗？
    _Tomorrow 2 PM is perfect_! | _What documents_ _do I need to bring_?

17. _Please bring_ _your passport_, _proof of income_, _and references_. | _If you like the apartment_, _we can process_ _the application immediately_.
    请带您的护照、收入证明和推荐信。如果您喜欢这个公寓，我们可以立即处理申请。

18. 好的，我会准备的。| 谢谢您的帮助！| 明天见！
    _Okay, I'll prepare them_. | _Thank you for your help_! | _See you tomorrow_!

#70196. Making Small Talk at a Party - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two people at a party where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are making small talk and getting to know each other. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there_! | _I don't think_ _we've met before_. | _I'm Sarah_. | _What's your name_?
    你好！我想我们之前没见过。我是莎拉。你叫什么名字？

2.  你好，莎拉！| 很高兴认识你。| 我叫李明，| 我是王先生的朋友。
    _Hello, Sarah_! | _Nice to meet you_. | _My name is Li Ming_, | _I'm Mr. Wang's friend_.

3.  _Nice to meet you_, _Li Ming_! | _How do you know_ _Mr. Wang_? | _He's my colleague_ _at work_.
    很高兴认识你，李明！你是怎么认识王先生的？他是我工作上的同事。

4.  我们是在语言交换活动中认识的。| 我教他中文，| 他教我英语。| 你们在一起工作多久了？
    _We met at_ _a language exchange event_. | _I teach him Chinese_, | _he teaches me English_. | _How long have you_ _worked together_?

5.  _We've been working_ _together for about_ _2 years now_. | _He's a great colleague_. | _How long have you_ _been learning English_?
    我们已经一起工作大约2年了。他是个很好的同事。你学英语多久了？

6.  我学英语已经3年了，| 但口语还是不太好。| 我很羡慕你的英语说得这么流利。
    _I've been learning English_ _for 3 years_, | _but my speaking_ _is still not very good_. | _I envy how fluently_ _you speak English_.

7.  _Thank you_, _but your English_ _is actually quite good_! | _I can understand_ _everything you're saying_. | _Practice makes perfect_.
    谢谢，但你的英语其实很好！我能理解你说的每一句话。熟能生巧。

8.  谢谢你的鼓励！| 我一直在努力练习。| 你以前去过中国吗？
    _Thank you for your encouragement_! | _I've been working hard_ _to practice_. | _Have you been to China before_?

9.  _Yes, I visited_ _Beijing and Shanghai_ _last year_. | _It was an amazing experience_. | _The food was incredible_.
    是的，我去年去过北京和上海。那是一次很棒的体验。食物很美味。

10. 太好了！| 你最喜欢什么中国菜？| 我猜你一定喜欢火锅。
    _That's great! What's your favorite_ _Chinese dish_? | _I bet you love_ _hot pot_.

11. _You're absolutely right_! | _I love hot pot_! | _I also enjoyed_ _dim sum and Peking duck_. | _What about you_?
    你完全正确！我喜欢火锅！我也喜欢点心和北京烤鸭。你呢？

12. 我喜欢川菜，| 特别是麻婆豆腐和宫保鸡丁。| 你喜欢辣的食物吗？
    _I like Sichuan cuisine_, | _especially Mapo Tofu_ _and Kung Pao Chicken_. | _Do you like spicy food_?

13. _I do like_ _some spicy food_, | _but not too hot_. | _I prefer mild_ _to medium spice levels_.
    我确实喜欢一些辣的食物，但不要太辣。我更喜欢温和到中等辣度。

14. 那下次我们可以一起去吃川菜，| 我推荐一些不太辣的菜。| 你觉得怎么样？
    _Then next time_ _we can go eat Sichuan food together_, | _I'll recommend_ _some less spicy dishes_. | _What do you think_?

15. _That sounds great_! | _I'd love to_ _try more Chinese food_. | _It's wonderful_ _to meet someone_ _who knows_ _the local cuisine_.
    听起来很棒！我很想尝试更多中国菜。遇到了解当地美食的人真是太好了。

16. 我也很高兴认识你！| 我们可以经常一起吃饭，| 这样我也可以练习英语。
    _I'm also very happy_ _to meet you_! | _We can often eat together_, | _so I can also practice English_.

17. _Perfect! This is going to be_ _a great friendship_. | _I'm looking forward to_ _our next meal together_.
    完美！这将是一段很棒的友谊。我期待我们下次一起吃饭。

18. 我也是！| 很高兴认识你，莎拉！
    _Me too! Nice to meet you_, _Sarah_!

#70195. Shopping for Groceries - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking supermarket staff member and a Mandarin-speaking customer who is shopping for groceries. They are discussing products, prices, and shopping assistance. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good morning_, _welcome to_ _Fresh Market_. | _How may I help you today_?
    早上好，欢迎光临新鲜市场。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好！我在找一些食材做晚饭。| 你能帮我找到鸡蛋和牛奶吗？
    _Hello! I'm looking for ingredients for dinner_. | _Can you help me find_ _eggs and milk_?

3.  _Of course! The dairy section_ _is over there_ _on the right_. | _Eggs and milk_ _are in the refrigerated area_.
    当然可以！乳制品区域在右边那边。鸡蛋和牛奶在冷藏区域。

4.  谢谢！| 我还需要一些蔬菜。| 你们有新鲜的菠菜吗？
    _Thank you! I also need some vegetables_. | _Do you have fresh spinach_?

5.  _Yes, we do_! | _The fresh vegetables_ _are in the produce section_ _at the back_. | _Spinach is on sale_ _this week_.
    是的，我们有！新鲜蔬菜在后面的农产品区域。这周菠菜在特价。

6.  太好了！| 菠菜多少钱一斤？| 还有其他蔬菜在特价吗？
    _Great! How much is spinach_ _per pound_? | _Are there other vegetables_ _on sale_?

7.  _Spinach is $2.99 per pound_ _this week_. | _We also have carrots_, _broccoli_, _and tomatoes_ _on special_.
    这周菠菜每磅2.99美元。我们还有胡萝卜、西兰花和西红柿在特价。

8.  我想买一些胡萝卜和西红柿。| 你们有有机蔬菜吗？
    _I'd like to buy_ _some carrots and tomatoes_. | _Do you have organic vegetables_?

9.  _Yes, we have_ _an organic section_ _in the produce area_. | _The organic vegetables_ _are a bit more expensive_, | _but they're pesticide-free_.
    是的，我们在农产品区域有有机区域。有机蔬菜稍微贵一些，但它们是农药免费的。

10. 我明白了。| 我还需要一些肉类。| 你们有新鲜的鸡肉吗？
    _I understand. I also need some meat_. | _Do you have fresh chicken_?

11. _Yes, we have_ _fresh chicken breasts_, _thighs_, _and whole chickens_. | _The chicken breasts_ _are $8.99 per pound_.
    是的，我们有新鲜的鸡胸肉、鸡腿和整只鸡。鸡胸肉每磅8.99美元。

12. 价格不错！| 我还需要一些调味料。| 你们有酱油和醋吗？
    _Good price! I also need some seasonings_. | _Do you have soy sauce and vinegar_?

13. _Yes, we have_ _a large selection_ _of Asian condiments_ _in aisle 5_. | _We carry_ _both Chinese and Japanese brands_.
    是的，我们在第5通道有大量亚洲调味料选择。我们销售中国和日本品牌。

14. 太好了！| 我还需要一些面条。| 你们有意大利面吗？
    _Great! I also need some noodles_. | _Do you have pasta_?

15. _Yes, we have_ _many types of pasta_ _in the pasta aisle_. | _Spaghetti_, _penne_, _and fettuccine_ _are all available_.
    是的，我们在意大利面通道有很多类型的意大利面。意大利细面、通心粉和宽面都有。

16. 完美！| 我想我找到所有需要的东西了。| 收银台在哪里？
    _Perfect! I think I've found_ _everything I need_. | _Where are the checkout counters_?

17. _The checkout counters_ _are at the front_ _of the store_. | _We have both_ _regular lanes_ _and self-checkout_. | _Which would you prefer_?
    收银台在商店前面。我们既有普通通道也有自助结账。您更喜欢哪个？

18. 我想用自助结账。| 谢谢你的帮助！
    _I'd like to use_ _self-checkout_. | _Thank you for your help_!

19. _You're welcome! Have a great day_! | _Come back soon_!
    不客气！祝您有愉快的一天！欢迎再来！

#70194. Discussing Weekend Plans - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two friends where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are discussing their plans for the upcoming weekend and suggesting activities to do together. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hey there_! | _What are your plans_ _for this weekend_? | _I'm looking for_ _something fun to do_.
    嘿！你这个周末有什么计划？我在找一些有趣的事情做。

2.  我还没有具体计划。| 你有什么想法吗？| 我想出去走走，| 不想整天待在家里。
    _I don't have_ _specific plans yet_. | _Do you have any ideas_? | _I want to go out_, | _don't want to stay home_ _all day_.

3.  _Great idea! I was thinking_ _we could go_ _to the new art museum_ _that just opened_. | _Have you heard about it_?
    好主意！我在想我们可以去刚开张的新艺术博物馆。你听说过吗？

4.  新艺术博物馆？| 在哪里？| 我还没听说过。
    _New art museum_? | _Where is it_? | _I haven't heard about it_.

5.  _It's downtown_, _near the central park_. | _They have_ _some amazing exhibitions_ _this month_. | _And admission is free_ _on weekends_.
    在市中心，靠近中央公园。他们这个月有一些很棒的展览。而且周末免费入场。

6.  免费入场？太好了！| 我们什么时候去？| 周六还是周日？
    _Free admission? That's great_! | _When should we go_? | _Saturday or Sunday_?

7.  _I think Saturday_ _would be better_. | _It's usually less crowded_ _than Sunday_. | _We could go_ _around 10 AM_.
    我觉得周六会更好。通常比周日人少。我们可以在上午10点左右去。

8.  上午10点很好！| 参观完博物馆后，| 我们还可以做什么？
    _10 AM is perfect_! | _After visiting the museum_, | _what else can we do_?

9.  _We could have lunch_ _at that new Italian restaurant_ _nearby_. | _I've heard_ _the food is excellent_. | _Then maybe_ _we could go shopping_.
    我们可以在附近那家新开的意大利餐厅吃午饭。我听说食物很棒。然后也许我们可以去购物。

10. 听起来很棒！| 我想买一些新衣服。| 你知道附近有什么好的购物中心吗？
    _Sounds great! I want to buy_ _some new clothes_. | _Do you know_ _any good shopping centers nearby_?

11. _Yes, there's_ _a great mall_ _just 2 blocks away_. | _They have_ _all the major stores_. | _We could spend_ _a few hours there_.
    是的，就在2个街区外有一个很棒的购物中心。他们有所有主要的商店。我们可以在那里花几个小时。

12. 太好了！| 这样我们就有完整的一天计划了。| 我们需要提前预订餐厅吗？
    _Great! So we have_ _a complete day planned_. | _Do we need to book_ _the restaurant in advance_?

13. _It's probably_ _a good idea_ _to make a reservation_. | _I can call them tomorrow_. | _What time would you like_ _to have lunch_?
    提前预订可能是个好主意。我明天可以打电话给他们。你想什么时候吃午饭？

14. 下午1点左右怎么样？| 这样我们有足够的时间参观博物馆。
    _How about_ _around 1 PM_? | _This gives us enough time_ _to visit the museum_.

15. _Perfect timing! I'll make_ _a reservation for 1 PM_. | _This is going to be_ _a fantastic weekend_.
    时间很完美！我会预订下午1点。这将是一个很棒的周末。

16. 我完全同意！| 我很期待。| 我们还需要准备什么吗？
    _I completely agree_! | _I'm looking forward to it_. | _Do we need to prepare_ _anything else_?

17. _Just bring_ _comfortable shoes_ _for walking_. | _And maybe_ _a camera_ _for the museum_. | _I'll bring_ _my credit card_ _for shopping_.
    只需要带舒适的步行鞋。也许还要带相机去博物馆。我会带信用卡去购物。

18. 好的！| 我会准备好的。| 周六上午10点见！
    _Okay! I'll be ready_. | _See you Saturday_ _at 10 AM_!

#70193. Ordering Coffee at a Café - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking barista and a Mandarin-speaking customer who wants to order coffee at a café. They are discussing coffee options, sizes, and preferences. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good morning_, _welcome to_ _Coffee Corner_! | _What can I get_ _for you today_?
    早上好，欢迎光临咖啡角！今天我能为您准备什么？

2.  你好！我想点一杯咖啡。| 你们有什么推荐的吗？
    _Hello! I'd like to order_ _a cup of coffee_. | _What do you recommend_?

3.  _Our most popular drink_ _is the caramel latte_. | _It's smooth and sweet_. | _We also have_ _a great cappuccino_.
    我们最受欢迎的饮品是焦糖拿铁。它很顺滑甜美。我们还有很棒的卡布奇诺。

4.  焦糖拿铁听起来不错！| 你们有不同的大小吗？
    _Caramel latte sounds good_! | _Do you have_ _different sizes_?

5.  _Yes, we have small, medium_, _and large_. | _The medium is_ _our most popular size_. | _What size would you like_?
    是的，我们有小杯、中杯和大杯。中杯是我们最受欢迎的尺寸。您想要什么尺寸？

6.  我要中杯吧。| 你们可以调整甜度吗？
    _I'll have medium, please_. | _Can you adjust_ _the sweetness_?

7.  _Absolutely! We can make_ _it less sweet or_ _add extra caramel_. | _How sweet_ _do you like it_?
    当然可以！我们可以让它不那么甜或添加额外的焦糖。您喜欢多甜？

8.  我喜欢不太甜的，| 所以请少放点糖浆。| 你们有脱脂牛奶吗？
    _I like it not too sweet_, | _so please put less syrup_. | _Do you have_ _skim milk_?

9.  _Yes, we have skim milk_, _whole milk, and almond milk_. | _Which would you prefer_?
    是的，我们有脱脂牛奶、全脂牛奶和杏仁奶。您更喜欢哪种？

10. 我要脱脂牛奶。| 总共多少钱？
    _I'll have skim milk_. | _How much is the total_?

11. _The medium caramel latte_ _with skim milk_ _is $4.50_. | _Would you like_ _anything else_ _with your coffee_?
    中杯焦糖拿铁配脱脂牛奶是4.50美元。您还要其他什么配咖啡吗？

12. 你们有什么糕点吗？| 我想配个甜点。
    _Do you have any pastries_? | _I'd like a dessert_ _to go with it_.

13. _We have fresh croissants_, _muffins, and cookies_. | _The chocolate chip cookies_ _are baked daily_.
    我们有新鲜的可颂、马芬和饼干。巧克力豆饼干是每天现烤的。

14. 我要一个巧克力豆饼干。| 这样总共多少钱？
    _I'll have a chocolate_ _chip cookie_. | _How much is the_ _total now_?

15. _Your total is $6.25_. | _Your order number is 42_. | _Please wait for your coffee_.
    您的总额是6.25美元。您的订单号是42。请等待您的咖啡。

16. 好的，谢谢！| 大概需要多长时间？
    _Okay, thank you_! | _How long will it take_?

17. _It should be ready_ _in about 5 minutes_. | _We'll call your number_ _when it's ready_.
    应该在大约5分钟内准备好。准备好时我们会叫您的号码。

18. 太好了！| 我可以在那边坐着等吗？
    _Great! Can I sit_ _over there to wait_?

19. _Of course! There are_ _some tables by the window_. | _We'll bring your order_ _to your table_.
    当然可以！窗边有一些桌子。我们会把您的订单送到您的桌子。

---

#70192. Asking for Help with Homework - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two students where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are discussing homework difficulties and helping each other with academic problems. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hey, Li Wei_! | _How's your homework going_? | _I'm stuck on the_ _math problems_.
    嘿，李伟！你的作业做得怎么样？我在数学题上卡住了。

2.  你好，汤姆！| 我的数学作业也遇到困难了。| 这些代数题太难了。
    _Hello, Tom! My math_ _homework is also difficult_. | _These algebra problems_ _are too hard_.

3.  _I know, right? I've been_ _working on them for hours_. | _Do you want to_ _study together_?
    我知道，对吧？我已经做了几个小时了。你想一起学习吗？

4.  好主意！| 两个人一起做会容易一些。| 我们可以互相帮助。
    _Great idea! It's easier when_ _two people work together_. | _We can help each other_.

5.  _Perfect! Let's start with_ _problem number 5_. | _I think I understand_ _the first part_.
    完美！我们从第5题开始。我想我理解第一部分。

6.  好的，让我看看第5题。| 这道题是关于二次方程的，对吗？
    _Okay, let me look_ _at problem 5_. | _This is about quadratic_ _equations, right_?

7.  _Yes, exactly! We need_ _to find the value_ _of x_. | _I got x equals 3_, _but I'm not sure_.
    是的，完全正确！我们需要找到x的值。我得到x = 3，但我不确定。

8.  让我检查一下你的答案。| 如果x = 3，| 那么代入原方程：3² + 2(3) - 15 = 0。
    _Let me check your answer_. | _If x equals 3_, | _then substitute into_ _the original equation_: _3² + 2(3) - 15 = 0_.

9.  _That's 9 + 6 - 15 = 0_, | _which equals 0_. | _So x equals 3 is correct_!
    那是9 + 6 - 15 = 0，等于0。所以x = 3是正确的！

10. 太好了！| 现在让我们做下一题。| 这道题看起来更复杂。
    _Great! Now let's do_ _the next problem_. | _This one looks more complicated_.

11. _You're right, this one_ _is harder_. | _It's about factoring polynomials_. | _Do you remember_ _how to do this_?
    你说得对，这道题更难。这是关于因式分解多项式的。你还记得怎么做吗？

12. 我记得一些，| 但不太确定。| 我们可以一起试试。
    _I remember some, but_ _I'm not sure_. | _We can try together_.

13. _Let's start by looking_ _for common factors_. | _I see we can_ _factor out an x_ _from each term_.
    让我们先寻找公因式。我看到我们可以从每一项中提取x。

14. 对！| 所以我们可以写成x(x² + 2x - 15)。| 现在括号里的部分可以进一步分解。
    _Right! So we can_ _write it as x(x² + 2x - 15)_. | _Now the part in_ _parentheses can be factored further_.

15. _Exactly! We need to_ _find two numbers that_ _multiply to -15 and_ _add to 2_.
    完全正确！我们需要找到两个数，它们相乘等于-15，相加等于2。

16. 让我想想...| 5和-3怎么样？| 5 × (-3) = -15，5 + (-3) = 2。
    _Let me think... How about_ _5 and -3_? | _5 × (-3) = -15_, _5 + (-3) = 2_.

17. _Perfect! So the answer_ _is x(x + 5)(x - 3)_. | _You're really good at this_!
    完美！所以答案是x(x + 5)(x - 3)。你真的很擅长这个！

18. 谢谢！| 我们一起做确实容易多了。| 我们继续做下一题吗？
    _Thank you! It's much_ _easier when we work together_. | _Should we continue_ _with the next problem_?

19. _Absolutely! I think we're_ _on a roll now_. | _Let's keep going_.
    当然！我想我们现在状态很好。让我们继续。

---

#70191. Discussing Travel Plans - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two friends where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are discussing their upcoming travel plans and sharing travel experiences. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hi there_! | _I heard you're planning_ _a trip to Japan_. | _Is that really true_?
    你好！我听说你计划去日本旅行。是真的吗？

2.  是的！我下个月要去日本。| 我很兴奋，这是我第一次去亚洲。
    _Yes! I'm going to_ _Japan next month_. | _I'm very excited_, _this is my first time_ _going to Asia_.

3.  _That's amazing! Japan is_ _a wonderful country_. | _Which cities are you_ _planning to visit_?
    太棒了！日本是一个很棒的国家。你计划访问哪些城市？

4.  我想去东京、京都和大阪。| 每个城市待3天。| 你有什么建议吗？
    _I want to go to_ _Tokyo, Kyoto, and Osaka_. | _Three days in each city_. | _Do you have any suggestions_?

5.  _That's a great itinerary_! | _Tokyo is amazing for_ _shopping and food_. | _Kyoto is perfect_ _for traditional culture_.
    这是很棒的行程！东京购物和美食很棒。京都传统文化很完美。

6.  我听说京都的寺庙很美。| 你有什么推荐的景点吗？
    _I heard the temples_ _in Kyoto are beautiful_. | _What attractions do you recommend_?

7.  _Absolutely! You must visit_ _the Golden Pavilion and_ _Fushimi Inari Shrine_. | _They're absolutely breathtaking_.
    当然！你必须参观金阁寺和伏见稻荷大社。它们令人叹为观止。

8.  我会把它们加入我的行程。| 关于交通，你有什么建议？
    _I'll add them to_ _my itinerary_. | _What about transportation, any suggestions_?

9.  _I recommend getting_ _a Japan Rail Pass_ _if you're traveling_ _between cities_. | _It's very cost-effective for_ _multiple trips_.
    如果你在城市间旅行，我建议买日本铁路通票。多次旅行很划算。

10. 好主意！| 我还需要预订酒店吗？| 还是可以用其他住宿方式？
    _That's a good idea_! | _Do I also need_ _to book hotels_? | _Or can I use_ _other accommodation options_?

11. _You have several options_: | _hotels, ryokans (traditional inns)_, _or Airbnb_. | _I stayed in a_ _ryokan in Kyoto_, _it was amazing_.
    你有几个选择：酒店、日式旅馆（传统客栈）或爱彼迎。我在京都住过日式旅馆，很棒。

12. 日式旅馆听起来很有趣！| 它们贵吗？| 需要提前预订吗？
    _Ryokans sound interesting_! | _Are they very expensive_? | _Do I need to_ _book in advance_?

13. _They can be expensive_, | _but the experience is_ _worth it_. | _Yes, you should book_ _at least 2-3 months ahead_.
    它们可能很贵，但体验值得。是的，你应该至少提前2-3个月预订。

14. 明白了。| 关于食物，你有什么推荐？| 我想尝试真正的日本料理。
    _I understand completely_. | _What about food, any_ _recommendations_? | _I want to try_ _real Japanese cuisine_.

15. _You must try sushi_, _ramen, and tempura_! | _Also, don't miss the_ _street food in Osaka_. | _It's absolutely incredible_.
    你必须尝试寿司、拉面和天妇罗！还有，不要错过大阪的街头小吃。很不可思议。

16. 听起来很美味！| 我需要学习一些日语吗？| 还是英语就够了？
    _That sounds delicious_! | _Do I need to_ _learn some Japanese_? | _Or is English enough_?

17. _Learning basic phrases_ _like "hello" and "thank you"_ _is helpful_. | _But in big cities_, _many people speak some English_.
    学习基本短语如"你好"和"谢谢"很有帮助。但在大城市，很多人会说一些英语。

18. 好的，我会学一些基本短语。| 还有什么其他建议吗？
    _Okay, I'll learn_ _some basic phrases_. | _Any other useful suggestions_?

19. _Just enjoy yourself completely_! | _Japan is very safe_ _and the people are friendly_. | _You'll have an amazing time_.
    只要享受自己！日本很安全，人们很友好。你会度过很棒的时光。

20. 谢谢你的建议！| 我真的很期待这次旅行。
    _Thank you for your suggestions_! | _I'm really looking forward_ _to this trip_.

#70190. Ordering Pizza Delivery - Business

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking pizza delivery staff member and a Mandarin-speaking customer who wants to order pizza for delivery. They are discussing pizza options, toppings, and delivery details. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good evening, welcome to_ _Pizza Palace_. | _How may I help you today_?
    晚上好，欢迎光临披萨宫殿。今天有什么可以为您效劳的吗？

2.  你好！我想订披萨外卖。| 你们现在还在营业吗？
    _Hello! I'd like to_ _order pizza for delivery_. | _Are you still open now_?

3.  _Yes, we're open_ _until 11 PM_. | _What kind of pizza_ _would you like_ _to order today_?
    是的，我们营业到晚上11点。您今天想订什么类型的披萨？

4.  我想订一个大披萨，| 可以自己选择配料吗？
    _I'd like to order_ _a large pizza_, | _can I choose_ _my own toppings_?

5.  _Absolutely! We have many_ _toppings to choose from_. | _What would you like_ _on your pizza_?
    当然可以！我们有很多配料可以选择。您想要什么配料？

6.  我要意大利香肠、蘑菇和青椒。| 你们有奶酪披萨吗？
    _I want pepperoni, mushrooms_, _and green peppers_. | _Do you have cheese pizza_?

7.  _Yes, we have several_ _cheese options_: | _mozzarella, cheddar, and parmesan_. | _Which would you prefer_?
    是的，我们有几种奶酪选择：马苏里拉、切达和帕尔马干酪。您更喜欢哪种？

8.  我要马苏里拉奶酪。| 披萨底是什么类型的？
    _I'll have mozzarella cheese_. | _What type of pizza_ _base do you have_?

9.  _We have thin crust_, _thick crust_, _and stuffed crust_. | _The thin crust is_ _our most popular_.
    我们有薄底、厚底和夹心底。薄底是我们最受欢迎的。

10. 我要薄底。| 大概需要多长时间？
    _I'll have thin crust_. | _How long will it take_?

11. _Delivery usually takes_ _30-45 minutes_. | _What's your delivery address_? | _I'll calculate the delivery fee_.
    外卖通常需要30-45分钟。您的地址是什么？我来计算外卖费。

12. 我的地址是123号主街，| 在市中心附近。| 外卖费是多少？
    _My address is 123 Main Street_, | _near the city center_. | _What's the delivery fee_?

13. _For your location, the_ _delivery fee is $3.50_. | _Your total will be_ _$18.50_. | _Does that sound correct_?
    对于您的位置，外卖费是3.50美元。您的总额将是18.50美元。听起来对吗？

14. 是的，价格正确。| 你们接受什么付款方式？
    _Yes, the price is correct_. | _What payment methods_ _do you accept_?

15. _We accept cash, credit_ _cards, and online payments_. | _You can pay_ _when the pizza arrives_.
    我们接受现金、信用卡和在线支付。您可以在披萨到达时付款。

16. 好的，我付现金。| 还有什么其他需要注意的吗？
    _Okay, I'll pay in cash_. | _Is there anything else_ _I should know_?

17. _Your order is confirmed_. | _Your order number is 5678_. | _We'll call you_ _when the driver_ _is on the way_.
    您的订单已确认。您的订单号是5678。司机上路时我们会打电话给您。

18. 太好了！| 谢谢你的帮助。| 我期待披萨的到来！
    _That's great! Thank you_ _for your help_. | _I'm looking forward to_ _the pizza arriving_!

19. _You're welcome_! | _Enjoy your pizza_! | _Thank you for choosing_ _Pizza Palace_.
    不客气！享受您的披萨！感谢您选择披萨宫殿。

#70189. Discussing Movies and Entertainment - Social

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between two friends where one is an English-speaking person and the other is a Mandarin-speaking person. They are discussing movies, TV shows, and entertainment preferences. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Hey there_! | _Have you seen_ _any good movies lately_? | _I'm looking for_ _something to watch_.
    嘿！你最近看过什么好电影吗？我在找一些东西看。

2.  我上周看了一部很棒的电影！| 叫《星际穿越》，| 是关于太空旅行的科幻片。
    _I watched a great movie_ _last week_! | _Called "Interstellar"_, | _it's a sci-fi film_ _about space travel_.

3.  _Oh, I love that movie_! | _It's one of my favorites_. | _What did you think_ _of the ending_?
    哦，我喜欢那部电影！它是我最喜欢的之一。你觉得结局怎么样？

4.  结局很感人，| 但有点复杂。| 我看了两遍才完全理解。
    _The ending was touching_, | _but a bit complicated_. | _I watched it twice_ _to fully understand_.

5.  _I agree_, _the ending_ _is quite complex_. | _Have you seen_ _any other Christopher Nolan movies_?
    我同意，结局很复杂。你看过其他克里斯托弗·诺兰的电影吗？

6.  没有，这是我第一次看他的电影。| 你推荐看哪一部？
    _No, this is my first time_ _watching his films_. | _Which one_ _do you recommend_?

7.  _I'd recommend_ _"Inception"_. | _It's also very complex_, | _but really interesting_. | _It's about_ _dreams and reality_.
    我推荐《盗梦空间》。它也很复杂，但很有趣。它是关于梦境和现实的。

8.  听起来很有趣！| 我还喜欢看动作片。| 你有什么推荐吗？
    _Sounds interesting_! | _I also like_ _action movies_. | _What do you recommend_?

9.  _For action movies_, _I love_ _"Mad Max: Fury Road"_. | _It's non-stop action_ _from start to finish_.
    对于动作片，我喜欢《疯狂的麦克斯：狂暴之路》。从头到尾都是不间断的动作。

10. 我听说过这部电影！| 它获得了很多奖项，对吗？
    _I've heard of this movie_! | _It won many awards_, _right_?

11. _Yes, it won_ _6 Academy Awards_! | _The action scenes_ _are incredible_. | _What about you_? | _What genres_ _do you enjoy_?
    是的，它获得了6项奥斯卡奖！动作场面令人难以置信。你呢？你喜欢什么类型？

12. 我喜欢喜剧和爱情片。| 最近有什么好的喜剧片吗？
    _I like comedies_ _and romantic films_. | _Are there any good comedies_ _recently_?

13. _I recently watched_ _"The Grand Budapest Hotel"_. | _It's a comedy_ _by Wes Anderson_. | _Very funny and clever_.
    我最近看了《布达佩斯大饭店》。这是韦斯·安德森的喜剧。很有趣很聪明。

14. 我会把它加入我的观看清单！| 关于电视剧，你有什么推荐吗？
    _I'll add it_ _to my watchlist_! | _What about TV shows_, _any recommendations_?

15. _I'm currently watching_ _"Breaking Bad"_. | _It's a drama_ _about a chemistry teacher_ _who becomes a drug dealer_. | _Very intense_.
    我目前在看《绝命毒师》。这是一部关于化学老师变成毒贩的剧。很紧张。

16. 我听说过这部剧！| 它很受欢迎，对吗？
    _I've heard of this show_! | _It's very popular_, _right_?

17. _Yes, it's considered_ _one of the best TV shows_ _ever made_. | _The acting_ _is amazing_. | _Have you seen_ _any Chinese TV shows_?
    是的，它被认为是史上最好的电视剧之一。演技很棒。你看过中国电视剧吗？

18. 我看过一些古装剧，| 比如《甄嬛传》。| 你喜欢看中国电影吗？
    _I've watched some_ _period dramas_, | _like "Empresses in the Palace"_. | _Do you like_ _Chinese movies_?

19. _I'd love to_ _watch more Chinese films_! | _Can you recommend_ _some good ones_? | _I'm interested_ _in learning_ _about Chinese culture_.
    我很想看更多中国电影！你能推荐一些好的吗？我对了解中国文化很感兴趣。

20. 当然可以！| 我推荐《霸王别姬》和《活着》。| 它们都是经典作品。
    _Of course_! | _I recommend "Farewell My Concubine"_ _and "To Live"_. | _They are both classics_.

#70188. A Low-score University Assignment - Education

Briefing: This dialogue is a conversation between an English-speaking university lecturer and a Mandarin-speaking student. They are discussing the student's poor grade on an assignment and how to improve academic writing. The dialogue begins now.

1.  _Good afternoon_! _Come in and take a seat please_. | _I received your email_ | _saying you wanted to meet me_.
    下午好！请进，请坐。| 我收到了你发的邮件，| 说你想跟我见面。

2.  您好。是的。| 谢谢您抽时间见我。
    _Hello_. _Yes_. | _Thank you for taking the time_ | _to see me_.

3.  _That's totally fine_. | _I try to leave some free time_ | _available each day for students_. | _I hope your studies_ | _are going well_.
    没关系。| 我每天都会尽量| 给学生留出些空余时间。| 希望你学习进展顺利。

4.  事实上，| 我对我第一篇论文的分数| 不是很满意。| 我不理解您为什么会| 给我这么低的分数。
    _In fact_, | _I'm not very satisfied with_ | _the grade I received_ | _for my first paper_. | _I don't understand_ | _why you gave me_ | _such a low score_.

5.  _Oh, right_. | _I wanted to have a talk with you_ | _about that_, | _but I just haven't had the chance_.
    哦，对。| 我本来就想和你| 谈谈这件事，| 只是一直没机会。

6.  我明白。| 希望您可以给我一些反馈。| 距离下一节课还有一小时，| 希望时间足够。
    _I understand_. | _I hope you can give me_ | _some feedback_. | _There's still an hour_ | _until the next class_, | _so I hope we have enough time_.

7.  _The reason your paper_ | _isn't as good as it could be_ | _is the structure_ | _of your essay_. | _Your ideas are fine_, | _but the paper lacks_ | _a clear logical flow_.
    你论文成绩不理想的原因| 在于文章的结构。| 你的观点没问题，| 但论文缺乏清晰的逻辑性。

8.  哦。| 我的论文里确实有几个部分| 是最后几分钟才写的，| 所以写得比较仓促。| 我担心涵盖不了| 题目的所有要求。
    _Oh_. | _There were indeed a few parts_ | _in my paper_ | _that I wrote_ | _in the final minutes_, | _so they ended up a bit rushed_. | _I was worried_ | _that I wouldn't cover_ | _all the requirements_ | _of the topic_.

9.  _I see_. | _That might explain_ | _why your arguments_ | _aren't set up well_. | _It's often not a good idea_ | _to keep reworking your paper_.
    我明白了。| 这或许能解释为什么| 你的论点组织得不够好。| 不断地反复修改论文| 往往不是个好主意。

10. 我确实有这么做。| 我发现这篇论文| 比我想象中要难写，| 因为需要涵盖很多内容。
    _I did keep reworking it_. | _I found that this paper_ | _was harder to write_ | _than I imagined_ | _because there was so much to cover_.

11. _It is indeed a complicated topic_. | _It's easy to lose direction_, | _especially for university-level assignments_.
    这个话题确实复杂。| 很容易迷失方向，| 尤其是大学程度的作业。

12. 这跟我的中学作业不太一样。| 我想取得好成绩，| 但我真的需要帮助。
    _It's not like_ | _my secondary school assignments_. | _I want to get good grades_, | _but I really need some help_.

13. _I know a teacher_ | _who offers great tutoring sessions_ | _on writing papers_ | _for first-year students_ | _every week_. | _I can give you the details_ | _if you're interested_.
    我认识一位老师，| 每周都会给大一新生| 进行论文写作辅导，| 效果很不错。| 如果你有兴趣，| 我可以把详细情况告诉你。

14. 好的，谢谢您。| 这听起来真是个好主意。| 我相信这会对我| 下一次写论文大有帮助。
    _Okay, thank you_. | _That sounds like a great idea_. | _I believe it will really help me_ | _improve my next paper_.
